PREFACE,
This edition
is
based
on the following
three palm leaf
manuscripts.
1.
*. Belonging to the
Palace
Library,
Trivan-
drum.
2,
*?r. Lent
by
Mr. Govinda
Pisharoti,
Kailasa-
puram, Vaikkarn.
8.
*T.
Do.
Srikumaran Moothathu, Ayankudi,
Kaduthuruthi,
The colophons in these manuscripts show that the name
of the commentary
is Vivaraiia, and its author Kudraj while
the following verses
at the end of the manuscript
*$r furnish
certain
facts
regarding
the
date and
nativity
of the com-
mentator.
TTRT
(?)
The manuscript ^ runs up to the end of
26th chapter,
It is
written on palm
leaves
in Malayalaiii
characters and
looks about three
centuries
old.
It
is almost
free
from
errors.
The commentary
in
this
manuscript unlike
in the
other tAvo mentions
the name
of the metre etc-
in the text.
The manuscript *r having
been
returned
to the owner
soon after transcription, no description is given here.
The manuscript
*T consists
of Vivara^a,
running up to
the end of the 24th udhyaya with only
a
Malayalam com-
mentary on the 25th.
The commentary on the 26th chapter
is
incomplete; and
at the end
of
the manuscript is found
fragment
of
a Malayalam
commentary on the
8th chapter.
It is
written on
palm leaves
in
Malayalam
characters-
It
is about two centuries old and is full of errors.
K. SiMBASiVA
